The benefits and convenience of mineral sprays are undisputed - you can all agree on that right? Mineral sprays come in various sizes, small ones are easy to bring to school, work, travel, and the main purpose is to moisturize/provide extra hydration to the skin anytime, anywhere. Famous and popular mineral sprays like Avene or Evian are spring water/mineral water types. I'm not saying these brands are not good because I'm currently using Avene and like it a lot.\n\nThe difference that made me choose to buy Caudalie Grape Water first (the first mist I've ever had) is that its spray contains 100% extract from organic grapes. Reading the promotional section, I must say it sounds very \"bombastic\" but looking at the back label, I see it says \"USDA Certified Biobased Product - 97%\"... so does this mean the product is only 97% pure extract from grapes? Simple non-colorful label with green tones (common color for Caudalie products since the brand focuses on skincare with grape extract).\n\n- Caudalie introduces this mineral spray as:\n + Containing 100% grape water and enriched with Polysaccharide (a natural moisturizing agent in skin that helps retain water and has high antioxidant properties - source: Paula\u2019s Choice) and mineral salts.\n + 100% extract directly from small grapes during harvest season, has a soothing, cooling and moisturizing effect on skin.\n\n - The product does not contain: Parabens, Sulfates and Phthalates.\n\n- Impressions: As I described at the beginning, mineral sprays don't have anything too flashy for me since their simple function is to provide extra hydration for the skin conveniently. I feel I like this Caudalie Grape Water spray more than other types because the grape extract makes me immediately think of the antioxidant effect for skin that grapes provide. Just from spraying I feel at least this type of water has some added superior effects over others (even if it doesn't contain 100% grape extract >.<) When spraying it feels like a fine mist, it's hard to detect the grape scent but in comparison with Avene, I can feel Caudalie Grape Water is slightly more refreshing (or maybe I'm too swayed by the \"100% extract from grapes\" claim ^^ ) The water droplets spray a little \"stronger\" than the Avene bottle but still super gentle on skin. Absorption is quite fast (almost instant) leaving skin feeling much more \"moist\".
